                  <hi rend="ital">A certain black bird,</hi> (TA,) <hi rend="ital">well known;</hi> (K, TA;) [the <hi rend="ital">corvus,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">crow;</hi>] <hi rend="ital">of which there are several species;</hi> [namely, the <hi rend="ital">raven, carrioncrow, rook, jackdaw, jay, magpie,</hi> &amp;c.:] and it was used as a proper name, which, as is said in a trad., he [i. e. Mohammad] changed, because the word implies the meaning of distance, and because it is the name of a foul bird: (TA:) the pl. (K.) When the Arabs characterize a land as fertile, they say, <foreign lang="ar">وَقَعَ فِى أَرْضٍ لَا يُطَيَّرُ غُرَابُهَا</foreign> <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  [<hi rend="ital">He lighted upon a land of which the crow will not be made to fly away;</hi> because of its abundant herbage: see also <foreign lang="ar">طَيَّرَ</foreign>]: and <foreign lang="ar">وَجَدَ ثَمَرَةَ الغُرَابِ</foreign> <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  [<hi rend="ital">He found the fruit of the crow</hi>]; because that bird seeks after and chooses the most excellent of fruits. (TA.) They also say, <foreign lang="ar">طَارَ غُرَابُ فُلَانٍ</foreign> <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  [<hi rend="ital">The crow of such a one flew away</hi>], meaning <hi rend="ital">the head of such a one became white,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">hoary.</hi> (A, TA. [See also a similar phrase below.]) Also, <foreign lang="ar">فُلَانٌ أَبْصَرُ مِنْ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">غُرَابٍ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">Such a one is more sharp-sighted than a crow</hi>]: and <foreign lang="ar">أَحْذَرُ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">more cautious</hi>]: and <foreign lang="ar">أَزْهَى</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">more proud</hi>]: and <foreign lang="ar">أَشْأَمُ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">more inauspicious</hi>]: &amp;c.: they say that this bird is more inauspicious than any other inauspicious thing upon the earth.       <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n31622-3" target="مُغَيْرِبَانٌ" n="3" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n31628"/></foreign> is a dim. formed from a word other than that which is its proper source of derivation; being as though formed from   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n31622-4" target="مَغْرِبَانٌ" n="4" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n31625"/></foreign>. (S, L. [Hence it seems that this last word as given above was unknown to, or not admitted by, the authors of these two works.])          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">مَغْرِبٌ</foreign> signifies also <hi rend="ital">Anything</hi> [meaning <hi rend="ital">any place</hi>] <hi rend="ital">that conceals, veils,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">covers, one:</hi> pl. <foreign lang="ar">مَغَارِبُ</foreign>, which is applied to the <hi rend="ital">lucking-places</hi> of wild animals.
